Profile





 Profile





"I have no special talent. I am only passionately curious," Albert Einstein










                                Dr. Suvadip Batabyal


Contact Details Assistant Professor,Dept. of Computer Science & Information Systems,BITS Pilani Hyderabad CampusJawahar Nagar,Secunderabad-500078. Personal Website:    https://sites.google.com/site/suvadipb1534/ Previous Employment1. NIT Uttarakhand, Assistant Professor, dept. of CSE, 2014-2016.2. Senior Research Fellow, Jadavpur University, 2011-2014.3. Tata Consultancy Services Ltd., Kolkata, 2007-2009. Qualifications:1. B.E., Information Technology, Jadavpur University, 2007.2. M.E., Software Engineering,  Jadavpur University, 2011.3. PhD., Jadavpur University, 2016. Email: sbatabyal@hyderabad.bits-pilani.ac.in

Publications





 Publications





"The world is a great gymnasium where we come to make ourselves strong." Swami Vivekananda










                                Publications


Journals:



G. Goudar and S. Batabyal, "Point of Congestion in Large Buffer Mobile Opportunistic Networks," in IEEE Communications Letters, vol. 24, no. 7, pp. 1586-1590, July 2020.


Surendra Singh, Suvadip Batabyal, Sachin Tripathi, “Security aware dynamic scheduling algorithm (SADSA) for real-time applications on grid,” Cluster Computing (Springer), July, 2019.


S. Batabyal, P. Bhaumik, S. Chattopadhyay and S. Misra, "Steady-State Analysis of Buffer Occupancy for Different Forwarding Strategies in Mobile Opportunistic Network," in IEEE Transactions on Vehicular Technology, vol. 68, no. 7, pp. 6951-6963, July 2019.


Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Mobility Models, Traces and Impact of Mobility on Opportunistic Routing Algorithms: A Survey,” in IEEE Communications Surveys & Tutorials, vol.17, no.3, pp.1679-1707, 2015.



Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Analysing social behaviour and message dissemination in human based delay tolerant network,” in Wireless Networks (Springer/ACM), Volume 21, Issue 2 (2015), Page 513-529



 Conferences
 


Surendra Singh, Suvadip Batabyal, Sachin Tripathi: Security aware dynamic scheduling algorithm (SADSA) for real-time applications on grid. Cluster Computing 23(2): 989-1005 (2020).
Suvadip Batabyal, Lovekush Sharma: A Quantum Pipeline for an Executable Quantum Instruction Set Architecture. ISVLSI 2020: 294-299
Suvadip Batabyal, Özgür Erçetin: Optimal Buffering for High Quality Video Streaming in D2D Underlay Networks. WCNC 2020: 1-7.
 Suvadip Batabyal, Kounteya Sarkar, "Realizing parallelism in quantum MISD architecture," in Proc. of the 16th ACM Intl. Conf. on Computing Frontiers (CF'2019), pp. 230-234, Alghero, Italy — April 30 - May 02, 2019. 
G. Goudar and S. Batabyal, "A Modified Balls-into-Bins Model for Expected Buffer Occupancy in Mobile Opportunistic Networks," 2019 15th International Wireless Communications & Mobile Computing Conference (IWCMC), Tangier, Morocco, 2019, pp. 1488-1493. 
G. Goudar and S. Batabyal, "Characterizing and Estimating Bulk Transfer Size in Mobile Opportunistic Network," 2019 IEEE 89th Vehicular Technology Conference (VTC2019-Spring), Kuala Lumpur, Malaysia, 2019, pp. 1-5. 
Siuli Roy, Somprakash Bandyopadhyay, Munmun Das, Suvadip Batabyal, Sankhadeep Pal, “Real Time Traffic Congestion Detection and Management using Active RFID and GSM Technology,” in proc. of the 10th International Conference on Intelligent Transport Systems Telecommunication(ITST’10).
Mandal, K.; Sen, A.; Chakraborty, A.; Roy, S.; Batabyal, S.; Bandyopadhyay, S.,“Road traffic congestion monitoring and measurement using active RFID and GSM technology,” in 14th Intl. IEEE Conference on Intelligent Transportation Systems (ITSC’11), 2011, vol., no., pp.1375-1379, 5-7 Oct. 2011.
Mandal, Koushik; Sen, Arindam; Chakraborty, Abhijnan; Roy, Siuli ;Batabyal, Suvadip; Bandyopadhyay, Somprakash, “Use of Active RFID and GSM Technology to Monitor and Measure Road Traffic Congestion,” in proc. of 2nd National Conference on Intelligent Transport System, 25-27 August 2011.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Optimizing the Green Signal Time for Road Traffic Congestion Management,” in proc. of 1st Conference of Transportation Research Group of India (CTRG’11), 7-10th December, 2011.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Improving Network Performance with Affinity based Mobility Model in Opportunistic Network,” in 11th IEEE Wireless Telecommunications Symposium (WTS’12), 2012, pp.1–7.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Information Gradient based Content Search Architecture for Mobile Opportunistic Network,” in proc. of 4th IEEE International Conference on Computing, Communication and Networking Technologies (ICCCNT’13), 2013, pp: 19-26.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “A Fundamental Traffic Management Strategy for Mobile Opportunistic Network,” in 2nd IEEE Intl. Conf. on Advances in Computing, Communications and Informatics (ICACCI’13), 2013, pp. 822–827.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Estimators for Global Information in Mobile Opportunistic Network,” in proc. of IEEE Advanced Networks and Telecommunications Systems (ANTS’13), 2013, pp. 1–6.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Delay-Overhead Trade-Offs in Mobile Opportunistic Networks using TTL based Restricted Flooding,” in proc. IEEE conf. on Applications and Innovations in Mobile Computing (AIMoC’14), 2014, pp. 9–14.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Analysis of social structure and routing in human based delay tolerant network,” in proc. of 17th ACM international conference on Modeling, analysis and simulation of wireless and mobile systems (MSWiM’14), 2014, pp. 169–176.
Surendra Singh, Sachin Tripathi, and Suvadip Batabyal, “Secured Dynamic Scheduling Algorithm for Real-Time Applications on Grid” in proc. of the 12th International Conference on Information Systems Security (ICISS-2016), pp. 283-300.

Awards & Recognitions





 Awards & Recognitions





"You can't cross the sea merely by standing and staring at the water." Rabindranath Tagore










                                Invited Speaker, Tutorials


Invited speaker: IEEE International Conference on Big Data Analytics and Computer Intelligence 24-27 April, 2017, Chirala, A.P. Topic: Delay-Tolerant Network: A new networking paradigm for heterogeneous networks with dynamic connectivity.Tutorial: IEEE Intl. Conf. on Advanced Networks and Telecommunication Systems (ANTS 2017), 17-20 December 2017, Bhubaneshwar, Odisha. Topic: Mobility Models and Impact of Mobility on Dynamic Networks.





                                Awards and Recognition


1. 2011: DST-PURSE (Promotion of University Research and Scientific Excellence), GOI, 2011–12. 2. 2011: Sponsorship by IARCS to attend and present paper at WTS, 2011, London, U.K. 3. 2012: UGC-BSR (Basic Scientific Research), Fellowship in Science for Meritorious Students, 2012–2014. 4. 2014: Sponsorship by IARCS to attend and present paper at MSWiM, 2014, Montreal, Canada. 5. 2019: TUBITAK Visiting Scientist Fellowship at Sabanci University, Turkey.

Profile





 Profile





"I have no special talent. I am only passionately curious," Albert Einstein










                                Dr. Suvadip Batabyal


Contact Details Assistant Professor,Dept. of Computer Science & Information Systems,BITS Pilani Hyderabad CampusJawahar Nagar,Secunderabad-500078. Personal Website:    https://sites.google.com/site/suvadipb1534/ Previous Employment1. NIT Uttarakhand, Assistant Professor, dept. of CSE, 2014-2016.2. Senior Research Fellow, Jadavpur University, 2011-2014.3. Tata Consultancy Services Ltd., Kolkata, 2007-2009. Qualifications:1. B.E., Information Technology, Jadavpur University, 2007.2. M.E., Software Engineering,  Jadavpur University, 2011.3. PhD., Jadavpur University, 2016. Email: sbatabyal@hyderabad.bits-pilani.ac.in

Publications





 Publications





"The world is a great gymnasium where we come to make ourselves strong." Swami Vivekananda










                                Publications


Journals:



G. Goudar and S. Batabyal, "Point of Congestion in Large Buffer Mobile Opportunistic Networks," in IEEE Communications Letters, vol. 24, no. 7, pp. 1586-1590, July 2020.


Surendra Singh, Suvadip Batabyal, Sachin Tripathi, “Security aware dynamic scheduling algorithm (SADSA) for real-time applications on grid,” Cluster Computing (Springer), July, 2019.


S. Batabyal, P. Bhaumik, S. Chattopadhyay and S. Misra, "Steady-State Analysis of Buffer Occupancy for Different Forwarding Strategies in Mobile Opportunistic Network," in IEEE Transactions on Vehicular Technology, vol. 68, no. 7, pp. 6951-6963, July 2019.


Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Mobility Models, Traces and Impact of Mobility on Opportunistic Routing Algorithms: A Survey,” in IEEE Communications Surveys & Tutorials, vol.17, no.3, pp.1679-1707, 2015.



Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Analysing social behaviour and message dissemination in human based delay tolerant network,” in Wireless Networks (Springer/ACM), Volume 21, Issue 2 (2015), Page 513-529



 Conferences
 


Surendra Singh, Suvadip Batabyal, Sachin Tripathi: Security aware dynamic scheduling algorithm (SADSA) for real-time applications on grid. Cluster Computing 23(2): 989-1005 (2020).
Suvadip Batabyal, Lovekush Sharma: A Quantum Pipeline for an Executable Quantum Instruction Set Architecture. ISVLSI 2020: 294-299
Suvadip Batabyal, Özgür Erçetin: Optimal Buffering for High Quality Video Streaming in D2D Underlay Networks. WCNC 2020: 1-7.
 Suvadip Batabyal, Kounteya Sarkar, "Realizing parallelism in quantum MISD architecture," in Proc. of the 16th ACM Intl. Conf. on Computing Frontiers (CF'2019), pp. 230-234, Alghero, Italy — April 30 - May 02, 2019. 
G. Goudar and S. Batabyal, "A Modified Balls-into-Bins Model for Expected Buffer Occupancy in Mobile Opportunistic Networks," 2019 15th International Wireless Communications & Mobile Computing Conference (IWCMC), Tangier, Morocco, 2019, pp. 1488-1493. 
G. Goudar and S. Batabyal, "Characterizing and Estimating Bulk Transfer Size in Mobile Opportunistic Network," 2019 IEEE 89th Vehicular Technology Conference (VTC2019-Spring), Kuala Lumpur, Malaysia, 2019, pp. 1-5. 
Siuli Roy, Somprakash Bandyopadhyay, Munmun Das, Suvadip Batabyal, Sankhadeep Pal, “Real Time Traffic Congestion Detection and Management using Active RFID and GSM Technology,” in proc. of the 10th International Conference on Intelligent Transport Systems Telecommunication(ITST’10).
Mandal, K.; Sen, A.; Chakraborty, A.; Roy, S.; Batabyal, S.; Bandyopadhyay, S.,“Road traffic congestion monitoring and measurement using active RFID and GSM technology,” in 14th Intl. IEEE Conference on Intelligent Transportation Systems (ITSC’11), 2011, vol., no., pp.1375-1379, 5-7 Oct. 2011.
Mandal, Koushik; Sen, Arindam; Chakraborty, Abhijnan; Roy, Siuli ;Batabyal, Suvadip; Bandyopadhyay, Somprakash, “Use of Active RFID and GSM Technology to Monitor and Measure Road Traffic Congestion,” in proc. of 2nd National Conference on Intelligent Transport System, 25-27 August 2011.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Optimizing the Green Signal Time for Road Traffic Congestion Management,” in proc. of 1st Conference of Transportation Research Group of India (CTRG’11), 7-10th December, 2011.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Improving Network Performance with Affinity based Mobility Model in Opportunistic Network,” in 11th IEEE Wireless Telecommunications Symposium (WTS’12), 2012, pp.1–7.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Information Gradient based Content Search Architecture for Mobile Opportunistic Network,” in proc. of 4th IEEE International Conference on Computing, Communication and Networking Technologies (ICCCNT’13), 2013, pp: 19-26.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “A Fundamental Traffic Management Strategy for Mobile Opportunistic Network,” in 2nd IEEE Intl. Conf. on Advances in Computing, Communications and Informatics (ICACCI’13), 2013, pp. 822–827.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Estimators for Global Information in Mobile Opportunistic Network,” in proc. of IEEE Advanced Networks and Telecommunications Systems (ANTS’13), 2013, pp. 1–6.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Delay-Overhead Trade-Offs in Mobile Opportunistic Networks using TTL based Restricted Flooding,” in proc. IEEE conf. on Applications and Innovations in Mobile Computing (AIMoC’14), 2014, pp. 9–14.
Suvadip Batabyal, Parama Bhaumik, “Analysis of social structure and routing in human based delay tolerant network,” in proc. of 17th ACM international conference on Modeling, analysis and simulation of wireless and mobile systems (MSWiM’14), 2014, pp. 169–176.
Surendra Singh, Sachin Tripathi, and Suvadip Batabyal, “Secured Dynamic Scheduling Algorithm for Real-Time Applications on Grid” in proc. of the 12th International Conference on Information Systems Security (ICISS-2016), pp. 283-300.

Awards & Recognitions





 Awards & Recognitions





"You can't cross the sea merely by standing and staring at the water." Rabindranath Tagore










                                Invited Speaker, Tutorials


Invited speaker: IEEE International Conference on Big Data Analytics and Computer Intelligence 24-27 April, 2017, Chirala, A.P. Topic: Delay-Tolerant Network: A new networking paradigm for heterogeneous networks with dynamic connectivity.Tutorial: IEEE Intl. Conf. on Advanced Networks and Telecommunication Systems (ANTS 2017), 17-20 December 2017, Bhubaneshwar, Odisha. Topic: Mobility Models and Impact of Mobility on Dynamic Networks.





                                Awards and Recognition


1. 2011: DST-PURSE (Promotion of University Research and Scientific Excellence), GOI, 2011–12. 2. 2011: Sponsorship by IARCS to attend and present paper at WTS, 2011, London, U.K. 3. 2012: UGC-BSR (Basic Scientific Research), Fellowship in Science for Meritorious Students, 2012–2014. 4. 2014: Sponsorship by IARCS to attend and present paper at MSWiM, 2014, Montreal, Canada. 5. 2019: TUBITAK Visiting Scientist Fellowship at Sabanci University, Turkey.
